       <div id="readme" class="readme boxed-group clearfix announce instapaper_body md"> 
        <h3> 
         <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-book" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
          <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M3 5h4v1H3V5zm0 3h4V7H3v1zm0 2h4V9H3v1zm11-5h-4v1h4V5zm0 2h-4v1h4V7zm0 2h-4v1h4V9zm2-6v9c0 .55-.45 1-1 1H9.5l-1 1-1-1H2c-.55 0-1-.45-1-1V3c0-.55.45-1 1-1h5.5l1 1 1-1H15c.55 0 1 .45 1 1zm-8 .5L7.5 3H2v9h6V3.5zm7-.5H9.5l-.5.5V12h6V3z" />
         </svg> README.md </h3> 
        <article class="markdown-body entry-content" itemprop="text">
         <h1><a id="user-content-lodash-v4174" class="anchor" href="#lodash-v4174" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>lodash v4.17.4</h1> 
         <p><a href="https://lodash.com/">Site</a> | <a href="https://lodash.com/docs">Docs</a> | <a href="https://github.com/lodash/lodash/wiki/FP-Guide">FP Guide</a> | <a href="https://github.com/lodash/lodash/blob/master/.github/CONTRIBUTING.md">Contributing</a> | <a href="https://github.com/lodash/lodash/wiki" title="Changelog, Roadmap, etc.">Wiki</a> | <a href="https://js.foundation/community/code-of-conduct">Code of Conduct</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/bestiejs">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://gitter.im/lodash/lodash">Chat</a></p> 
         <p>The <a href="https://lodash.com/">Lodash</a> library exported as a <a href="https://github.com/umdjs/umd">UMD</a> module.</p> 
         <p>Generated using <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/lodash-cli">lodash-cli</a>:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-shell">
          <pre>$ npm run build
$ lodash -o ./dist/lodash.js
$ lodash core -o ./dist/lodash.core.js</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-download" class="anchor" href="#download" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Download</h2> 
         <ul> 
          <li><a href="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/lodash/lodash/4.17.4/dist/lodash.core.js">Core build</a> (<a href="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/lodash/lodash/4.17.4/dist/lodash.core.min.js">~4 kB gzipped</a>)</li> 
          <li><a href="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/lodash/lodash/4.17.4/dist/lodash.js">Full build</a> (<a href="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/lodash/lodash/4.17.4/dist/lodash.min.js">~24 kB gzipped</a>)</li> 
          <li><a href="https://www.jsdelivr.com/projects/lodash">CDN copies</a></li> 
         </ul> 
         <p>Lodash is released under the <a href="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/lodash/lodash/4.17.4/LICENSE">MIT license</a> &amp; supports modern environments.<br> Review the <a href="https://github.com/lodash/lodash/wiki/build-differences">build differences</a> &amp; pick one that’s right for you.</p> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" href="#installation" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Installation</h2> 
         <p>In a browser:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic">
          <pre>&lt;<span class="pl-ent">script</span> <span class="pl-e">src</span>=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>lodash.js<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>&gt;&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">script</span>&gt;</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>Using npm:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-shell">
          <pre>$ npm i -g npm
$ npm i --save lodash</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>In Node.js:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Load the full build.</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> _ <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>lodash<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Load the core build.</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> _ <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>lodash/core<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Load the FP build for immutable auto-curried iteratee-first data-last methods.</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> fp <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>lodash/fp<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Load method categories.</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> array <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>lodash/array<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">var</span> object <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>lodash/fp/object<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Cherry-pick methods for smaller browserify/rollup/webpack bundles.</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> at <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>lodash/at<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">var</span> curryN <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>lodash/fp/curryN<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong><br> Install <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/n_">n_</a> for Lodash use in the Node.js &lt; 6 REPL.</p> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-why-lodash" class="anchor" href="#why-lodash" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Why Lodash?</h2> 
         <p>Lodash makes JavaScript easier by taking the hassle out of working with arrays,<br> numbers, objects, strings, etc. Lodash’s modular methods are great for:</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li>Iterating arrays, objects, &amp; strings</li> 
          <li>Manipulating &amp; testing values</li> 
          <li>Creating composite functions</li> 
         </ul> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-module-formats" class="anchor" href="#module-formats" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Module Formats</h2> 
         <p>Lodash is available in a <a href="https://lodash.com/custom-builds">variety of builds</a> &amp; module formats.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/lodash">lodash</a> &amp; <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/browse/keyword/lodash-modularized">per method packages</a></li> 
          <li><a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/lodash-es">lodash-es</a>, <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/babel-plugin-lodash">babel-plugin-lodash</a>, &amp; <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/lodash-webpack-plugin">lodash-webpack-plugin</a></li> 
          <li><a href="https://github.com/lodash/lodash/tree/npm/fp">lodash/fp</a></li> 
          <li><a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/lodash-amd">lodash-amd</a></li> 
         </ul> 
        </article>
